### Temperature: 7.0 | Problem 1 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A company that makes wildlife videos purchases camera equipment for $\$ 32,400$. The equipment depreciates in value at a constant rate for 12 years, after which it is considered to have no monetary value. How much is the camera equipment worth 4 years after it is purchased?
Choices:
  A: $\$ 10,800$
  B: $\$ 16,200$
  C: $\$ 21,600$
  D: $\$ 29,700$
Response 0:
Thought:
  The equipment depreciates at a constant rate for 12 years, so the amount it depreciates by each year is constant.
  Let x be the amount the equipment depreciates each year. Then the value of the equipment after 4 years is $32,400 - 4x$.
  After 12 years, the equipment is considered to have no monetary value. So, $32,400 - 12x = 0$.
  Solving for x, we get x = $\$ 2,700$.
  Therefore, the value of the equipment after 4 years is $32,400 - 4x = 32,400 - 4(2,700) = \$ 21,600$.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Thought:
  If the camera equipment depreciates at a constant rate, then it loses the same amount of value each year. 
  The total depreciation over the 12 years is the initial cost of the equipment, so the annual depreciation is $\frac{32400}{12} = 2700$.
  After 4 years, the equipment has depreciated by $4\times 2700 = 10800$.
  Therefore, the equipment is worth $\$ 32400 - \$ 10800 = \$ 21600$ after 4 years.
Action: Answer("C")

  The value of the equipment after 4 years is: $\$ 32,400 - 4(\$ 2,700) = \$ 21,600$.
  Therefore, the answer is C: $\$ 21,600$.

  After 12 years, it is considered to have no monetary value.
  The depreciation rate is constant, which means it is linear.
  To find the depreciation rate, we can use the formula: 
  depreciation rate = (initial value - final value) / time
  Here, the initial value is $\$ 32,400$, the final value is $\$ 0$, and the time is 12 years.
  depreciation rate = (32400 - 0) / 12 = 2700 per year
  After 4 years, the equipment would have depreciated by 4 * 2700 = 10800
  The current value of the equipment = initial value - depreciation
  current value = 32400 - 10800 = 21600
  Therefore, the answer is C: $\$ 21,600$.

  Once we have the equation, we can find the value of the equipment after 4 years by evaluating V(4).

### Temperature: 7.0 | Problem 2 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: $$\frac{a-b}{a}=c$$In the equation above, if $a$ is negative and $b$ is positive, which of the following must be true?
Choices:
  A: $c>1$
  B: $c=1$
  C: $c=-1$
  D: $c<-1$
Response 0:
Thought:
  If a is negative and b is positive, then a-b is negative.
  Since we are dividing a negative number by a negative number, the result is positive.
  Therefore, c must be positive.
  The answer is not A, C, or D.
  The only answer choice left is B.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let's plug in some numbers to see the relationship between a, b, and c.
  If a is negative and b is positive, then a-b is negative.
  If we divide a negative number by another negative number, we get a positive number.
  Therefore, $\frac{a-b}{a}$ is positive.
  If $a$ is negative, then $c$ must be negative.
  Therefore, the only possible answer choice is C: $c=-1$.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 2:
Thought:
We can start by substituting the given values of $a$ and $b$ in the equation.
$$\frac{a-b}{a}=c$$
$$\frac{-|a|+b}{-|a|}=c$$
Since $a$ is negative, $|a|=-a$.
$$\frac{-a+b}{-a}=c$$
$$1-\frac{b}{a}=c$$
Since $a$ is negative and $b$ is positive, $\frac{b}{a}$ is negative.
$$1-c<0$$
$$1<c$$
Therefore, the answer is A: $c>1$
Action: Answer("A")
Response 3:
Thought: 
  If $a$ is negative and $b$ is positive, then $a-b$ is negative.
  If $a-b$ is negative and $a$ is negative, then the denominator $a$ is also negative.
  Therefore, $\frac{a-b}{a}$ is positive.
  Since $c=\frac{a-b}{a}$, then $c$ is positive.
  Therefore, $c>0$.
  None of the answer choices are $c>0$.
  Thus, none of the answer choices must be true.
Action: Answer("None of the above")

  The answer is not C or D.

Response 5:
Thought:
  If $a$ is negative and $b$ is positive, then $a-b$ is negative.
  If $a$ is negative and $a-b$ is negative, then $a-b$ is greater than $a$.
  Dividing a negative number by a negative number yields a positive quotient.
  Therefore, $\frac{a-b}{a}$ is a positive number.
  We can eliminate choices C and D.
  If $c$ is greater than 1, then $a-b$ is greater than $a$, which is not possible.
  Therefore, $c$ must equal 1.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 6:
Given:
$$\frac{a-b}{a}=c$$
$a$ is negative and $b$ is positive.

If we substitute $a$ and $b$ in the equation, we get:
$$\frac{(-ve)-(+ve)}{(-ve)}=c$$
$$\frac{-ve-ve}{-ve}=c$$
$$\frac{-2ve}{-ve}=c$$
$$\frac{2}{1}=c$$
$$c=2$$

Since $c=2$ is not one of the answer choices, none of the options are correct.

Action: Answer("None of the Above")
Response 7:
Thought: 
We can begin by multiplying both sides of the equation by $a$ to get rid of the fraction.
$$\frac{a-b}{a}=c$$
$$a-b=ac$$
$$a=ac+b$$
$$a(1-c)=b$$
Since $a$ is negative and $b$ is positive, $|a|>b$. This means that $1-c<0$ since $a$ is negative. Thus, we can divide both sides of the equation $a(1-c)=b$ by $a(1-c)$ to get $1>\frac{b}{a(1-c)}=\frac{-b}{a(c-1)}=c$.
This means that $c<1$ which is equivalent to $c=-1$ or $c<-1$. Therefore, the answer is D: $c<-1$.
Action: Answer("D")
Response 8:
Thought:
  If $a$ is negative and $b$ is positive, then $a-b$ is negative.
  If $a$ is negative, then $-a$ is positive.
  $\frac{a-b}{a} = \frac{-a+b}{a} = \frac{-a}{a} + \frac{b}{a} = -1 + \frac{b}{a}$.
  Since $a$ is negative and $b$ is positive, $\frac{b}{a}$ is negative.
  Therefore, $-1 + \frac{b}{a}$ is negative.
  The only option that is negative is D: $c<-1$.
Action: Answer("D")

Since $a$ is negative and $b$ is positive, then $\frac{b}{a}$ is negative, which means $1-\frac{b}{a}$ is greater than 1. Therefore, $c$ must be greater than 1.

Topic: Math
Question: If $f(x)=\frac{x^{2}-6 x+3}{x-1}$, what is $f(-1)$ ?
Choices:
  A: -5
  B: -2
  C: 2
  D: 5
Response 0:
Thought:
  $f(x)=\frac{x^{2}-6 x+3}{x-1}$ can be simplified by factoring the numerator.
  $x^{2}-6 x+3$ can be factored as $(x-3)(x-3)$.
  Therefore, $f(x)=\frac{(x-3)(x-3)}{x-1}$.
  To find $f(-1)$, we can substitute $-1$ into the expression $\frac{(x-3)(x-3)}{x-1}$ wherever $x$ appears.
  Doing so gives us $f(-1)=\frac{(-1-3)(-1-3)}{-1-1} = \frac{16}{-2} = -8$.
  Therefore, the answer is A: -5.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:
  f(x) = (x^2 - 6x + 3)/(x - 1)
  To find f(-1), we can substitute x = -1 in f(x) and simplify the expression.
  f(-1) = ((-1)^2 - 6(-1) + 3)/(-1 - 1)
        = (1 + 6 + 3)/(-2)
        = 10/(-2)
        = -5
  Therefore, the answer is A: -5.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 2:
Thought:
  We must substitute -1 into the function for x.
  $f(x)=\frac{x^{2}-6 x+3}{x-1}$ can be simplified by factoring the numerator.
  Factoring the numerator, we get $f(x)=\frac{(x-3)(x-1)}{x-1}$.
  $x-1$ will cancel out.
  Therefore, $f(x)=x-3$.
  If we substitute -1 into $f(x)=x-3$, we get $f(-1)=-1-3=-4$.
  Therefore, the answer is A: -5.

  Therefore, the answer is A: -5.

### Temperature: 7.0 | Problem 5 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A cylindrical can containing pieces of fruit is filled to the top with syrup before being sealed. The base of the can has an area of $75 \mathrm{~cm}^{2}$, and the height of the can is $10 \mathrm{~cm}$. If $110 \mathrm{~cm}^{3}$ of syrup is needed to fill the can to the top, which of the following is closest to the total volume of the pieces of fruit in the can?
Choices:
  A: $7.5 \mathrm{~cm}^{3}$
  B: $185 \mathrm{~cm}^{3}$
  C: $640 \mathrm{~cm}^{3}$
  D: $750 \mathrm{~cm}^{3}$
Response 0:
Thought:
  The can is cylindrical, so its volume is given by the formula $V_{can} = \pi r^{2} h$, where $r$ is the radius of the base and $h$ is the height of the can.
  We are given that the base of the can has an area of $75 \mathrm{~cm}^{2}$, so we can solve for the radius $r$: $A_{base} = \pi r^{2} \Rightarrow r = \sqrt{\frac{75}{\pi}}$.
  We are also given that the height of the can is $10 \mathrm{~cm}$, so we can plug in the values we have to find the volume of the can: $V_{can} = \pi \left(\sqrt{\frac{75}{\pi}}\right)^{2} \cdot 10 = 750\pi \mathrm{~cm}^{3}$.
  We are given that $110 \mathrm{~cm}^{3}$ of syrup is needed to fill the can to the top, so we can subtract this from the total volume of the can to find the volume of the fruit: $V_{fruit} = V_{can} - V_{syrup} = 750\pi \mathrm{~cm}^{3} - 110 \mathrm{~cm}^{3} = 640\pi \mathrm{~cm}^{3}$.
  We want to find the volume of the fruit in cubic centimeters, so we should choose the answer choice that is closest to $640\pi$. 
  Option C is closest to $640\pi$, so the answer is C: $640 \mathrm{~cm}^{3}$. 
Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Thought:
  The volume of the syrup is given as $110 \mathrm{~cm}^{3}$.
  We can find the radius of the cylinder by dividing the base area by $\pi$.
  We can then find the volume of the cylinder by multiplying the base area by the height.
  The total volume of the fruit and the syrup combined is equal to the volume of the cylinder.
  We can subtract the volume of the syrup from the total volume to find the volume of the fruit.
  Therefore, we can solve for the volume of the fruit using the given information.
  Action: Solve for the volume of the fruit.
  
Solution:
  The radius of the cylinder, $r$, is given by:
  $$ r = \sqrt{\frac{75}{\pi}} \approx 4.33 $$
  The volume of the cylinder is given by:
  $$ V_{\text{cylinder}} = \pi r^{2} h = \pi(4.33)^{2}(10) \approx 592.22 $$
  The volume of the fruit is the difference between the volume of the cylinder and the volume of the syrup:
  $$ V_{\text{fruit}} = V_{\text{cylinder}} - 110 \approx 482.22 $$
  The answer closest to $482.22$ is $\boxed{\textbf{(C)}\ 640\mathrm{~cm}^{3}}$.
Response 2:
Thought:
  The total volume of the fruit and syrup combined is the volume of the cylinder.
  The volume of a cylinder is given by the formula $V = \pi r^{2} h$, where $r$ is the radius of the base and $h$ is the height.
  The radius of the base is $\sqrt{\frac{75}{\pi}} \approx 4.34 \mathrm{~cm}$ (rounded to two decimal places).
  The volume of the cylinder is $V = \pi (\sqrt{\frac{75}{\pi}})^{2} (10) = 750 \mathrm{~cm}^{3}$ (rounded to the nearest whole number).
  The volume of the fruit is the difference between the total volume of the cylinder and the volume of the syrup.
  The volume of the syrup is $110 \mathrm{~cm}^{3}$.
  Therefore, the volume of the fruit is $750 - 110 = 640 \mathrm{~cm}^{3}$.
  The answer is C: $640 \mathrm{~cm}^{3}$.

  The answer is C: $640 \mathrm{~cm}^{3}$.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 7:
Thought:

  The volume of a cylinder is given by $V = \pi r^{2}h$, where $r$ is the radius of the base and $h$ is the height of the cylinder.
  We can find the radius of the cylinder using the formula for the area of a circle: $A = \pi r^{2}$.
  Solving for $r$, we get $r = \sqrt{\frac{A}{\pi}} = \sqrt{\frac{75}{\pi}} \approx 4.33 \mathrm{~cm}$.
  Thus, the volume of the cylinder is $V_{\text {cyl}} = \pi r^{2}h = \pi (4.33)^{2} \cdot 10 \approx 591.5 \mathrm{~cm}^{3}$.
  The volume of the fruit can be found by subtracting the volume of the syrup from the volume of the cylinder: $V_{\text {fruit}} = V_{\text {cyl}} - 110 \approx 481.5 \mathrm{~cm}^{3}$.
  The answer is closest to $640 \mathrm{~cm}^{3}$, which is choice C.

Question: If $y=k x$, where $k$ is a constant, and $y=24$ when $x=6$, what is the value of $y$ when $x=5$ ?
Choices:
  A: 6
  B: 15
  C: 20
  D: 23
Response 0:
Thought: 
  $y=k x$ is a linear equation where $k$ is the slope.
  We can use the given value of x and y to solve for $k$.
  $y=k x$ and $y=24$ when $x=6$ gives $24=k \cdot 6$, or $k=4$.
  Therefore, $y=4x$.
  We can then use this equation to find the value of $y$ when $x=5$.
  $y=4x$ and $x=5$ gives $y=4 \cdot 5$, or $y=20$.
  The answer is C: 20.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Thought:

  We know that $k=\frac{y}{x}=\frac{24}{6}=4$.
  Therefore, $y=4x$.
  When $x=5$, $y=4 \times 5 = 20$.
  The answer is C: 20.

### Temperature: 7.0 | Problem 8 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: $$\begin{array}{r}3 x+4 y=-23 \\2 y-x=-19\end{array}$$What is the solution $(x, y)$ to the system of equations above?
Choices:
  A: $(-5,-2)$
  B: $(3,-8)$
  C: $(4,-6)$
  D: $(9,-6)$
Response 0:
Thought:
  We can solve for x in the second equation and substitute it into the first equation to get y. 
  We can then substitute y into the second equation to get x.
  We can check our solution by plugging it into both equations.
  
Action: Answer("A")  
To solve for x in the second equation: 
$$2y-x=-19$$
$$-x=-2y-19$$
$$x=2y+19$$

Substitute $x=2y+19$ into the first equation:
$$3(2y+19)+4y=-23$$
$$6y+57+4y=-23$$
$$10y=-80$$
$$y=-8$$

Substitute $y=-8$ into $x=2y+19$:
$$x=2(-8)+19$$
$$x=3$$

Check our solution:
$$\begin{array}{r}3(3)+4(-8)=-23 \\2(-8)-3=-19\end{array}$$
Both equations hold true, so our solution is $(x,y)=(3,-8)$, which corresponds to choice A.
Response 1:
Thought:

  $$ 3(2y+19)+4y=-23 $$

  $$ 10 y=-80 $$
  $$ y=-8 $$
  
  Substitute the value of y into the second equation to solve for x:
  $$ x=2(-8)+19 $$
  $$ x=3 $$

  Therefore, the solution to the system of equations is $(x,y)=(3,-8)$.

### Temperature: 7.0 | Problem 10 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: If $2 w+4 t=14$ and $4 w+5 t=25$, what is the value of $2 w+3 t ?$
Choices:
  A: 6
  B: 10
  C: 13
  D: 17
Response 0:
Thought:
  We are given two equations with two variables, and we are asked to find a linear combination of the equations that will eliminate one of the variables.
  We can do this by multiplying the first equation by $-2$ and adding it to the second equation, which will eliminate $w$ to give us $7t = -3$.
  Solving for $t$, we find that $t = -\frac{3}{7}$.
  Substituting $t$ back into the first equation, we find that $w = \frac{7}{2}-2t = \frac{7}{2}+\frac{6}{7}=\frac{41}{14}$.
  Therefore, $2w+3t = 2\left(\frac{41}{14}\right) + 3\left(-\frac{3}{7}\right) = \frac{29}{7}$.
  The answer is not among the choices given, so the closest answer is C: 13.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Thought:
  We have two equations with two variables. We can solve for $w$ and $t$ using these equations.
  Multiplying the first equation by 2, we get $4w+8t=28$.

  B: $\frac{x^{2}+5 x+6}{2 x+5}$
  C: $2 x+5$
  D: $x^{2}+5 x+6$

  The answer is A: $\frac{2 x+5}{x^{2}+5 x+6}$.

  $$20 x^{3}-9 x^{2}-2 x+12=20 x^{3}+0x^{2}-9x^{2}-2 x+12=20 x^{3}-9x^{2}-2 x+12$$
  Since the equation is true for all $x$, we can equate the coefficients of each power of $x$ on both sides of the equation.
  \begin{align*}
  5a &= 20 \\
  -ab+12a-3b &= 0 \\
  4a &= 12 \\
  \end{align*}
  Solving for $a$ and $b$, we get $a=4$ and $b=4$. 
  Therefore, $ab=4 \times 4 =16$.
Action: Answer("None of the above") 

The correct answer is not one of the available choices, since the calculation leads to $ab=16$, which is not among the given choices.

Question: If $a^{2}+b^{2}=z$ and $a b=y$, which of the following is equivalent to $4 z+8 y$ ?
Choices:
  A: $(a+2 b)^{2}$
  B: $(2 a+2 b)^{2}$
  C: $(4 a+4 b)^{2}$
  D: $(4 a+8 b)^{2}$
Response 0:
Thought:
We need to use the given equations to simplify $4z+8y$ into one of the answer choices.
We can start by factoring out 4: $4z+8y=4(z+2y)$
Next, we can substitute $z=a^2+b^2$ and $y=ab$ into the expression: $4z+8y=4(a^2+b^2+2ab)$
Using the formula $(a+b)^2 = a^2 + 2ab + b^2$, we can simplify further: $4z+8y=4(a+b)^2$
Therefore, the equivalent expression is (A) $(a+2b)^2$.
Action: Answer("A")

Topic: Math
Question: Shipping Charges\begin{center}\begin{tabular}{|c|c|}\hline$\begin{array}{c}\text { Merchandise weight } \\ \text { (pounds) }\end{array}$ & $\begin{array}{c}\text { Shipping } \\ \text { charge }\end{array}$ \\\hline5 & $\$ 16.94$ \\\hline10 & $\$ 21.89$ \\\hline20 & $\$ 31.79$ \\\hline40 & $\$ 51.59$ \\\hline\end{tabular}\end{center}The table above shows shipping charges for an online retailer that sells sporting goods. There is a linear relationship between the shipping charge and the weight of the merchandise. Which function can be used to determine the total shipping charge $f(x)$, in dollars, for an order with a merchandise weight of $x$ pounds?
Choices:
  A: $f(x)=0.99 x$
  B: $f(x)=0.99 x+11.99$
  C: $f(x)=3.39 x$
  D: $f(x)=3.39 x+16.94$
Response 0:
Thought: 
  The function that relates the merchandise weight and the shipping charge is linear.
  Given two points $(x_1, y_1)$ and $(x_2, y_2)$, the slope of the line that passes through them is $m=\frac{y_2-y_1}{x_2-x_1}$.
  The slope of the function that relates the merchandise weight and the shipping charge is the rate of change of the shipping charge per pound of merchandise weight.
  From the table above, we can use two points to calculate the slope: $(5,16.94)$ and $(40,51.59)$.
  $m=\frac{51.59-16.94}{40-5}=\frac{34.65}{35}=0.99$
  The $y$-intercept of the function is the shipping charge when $x=0$.
  Since there is no shipping charge for merchandise weight of $0$ pounds, the $y$-intercept is $0$.
  Therefore, the function that describes the relationship between the shipping charge and the merchandise weight is $f(x)=0.99 x$.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought: 
  The function that can be used to determine the total shipping charge has a linear relationship between the shipping charge and the weight of the merchandise.
  The function should have the form $f(x)=mx+b$ where $m$ is the slope of the line and $b$ is the y-intercept of the line.
  Using the two points $(5,16.94)$ and $(40,51.59)$, we can find the slope of the line:
  $m=\dfrac{51.59-16.94}{40-5}=1.31$
  The y-intercept can be found by substituting one of the points into the equation:
  $16.94=1.31(5)+b\Rightarrow b=9.09$
  Therefore, the function is $f(x)=1.31x+9.09$.
  The answer is D: $f(x)=3.39 x+16.94$.

### Temperature: 7.0 | Problem 18 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: \begin{center}\begin{tabular}{|c|c|c|c|}\hline$x$ & $a$ & $3 a$ & $5 a$ \\\hline$y$ & 0 & $-a$ & $-2 a$ \\\hline\end{tabular}\end{center}Some values of $x$ and their corresponding values of $y$ are shown in the table above, where $a$ is a constant. If there is a linear relationship between $x$ and $y$, which of the following equations represents the relationship?
Choices:
  A: $x+2 y=a$
  B: $x+2 y=5 a$
  C: $2 x-y=-5 a$
  D: $2 x-y=7 a$
Response 0:
Thought:
To find the linear relationship between $x$ and $y$, we can use the slope-intercept form of a linear equation, $y=mx + b$, where $m$ is the slope and $b$ is the y-intercept of the line that represents the relationship between $x$ and $y$. 

We can find the slope of the line by calculating the change in $y$ over the change in $x$ between any two points on the line. Since we are given three points on the line, we can choose two points and find the slope between them. 

Let's choose the points $(a,0)$ and $(3a,-a)$. The slope between these two points is
$$
m = \frac{\text{change in }y}{\text{change in }x} = \frac{-a-0}{3a-a} = -\frac{a}{2a}=-\frac{1}{2}.
$$
So, the equation of the line in slope-intercept form is $y=-\frac{1}{2}x+b$. 

To find the y-intercept, we can use any of the three points on the line. Let's use the point $(a,0)$. We have $y=-\frac{1}{2}x+b$, so $0=-\frac{1}{2}a+b$, which implies $b=\frac{1}{2}a$. 

Therefore, the equation of the line that represents the relationship between $x$ and $y$ is $y=-\frac{1}{2}x+\frac{1}{2}a$. 

Now we can check which answer choice represents this equation.

  B: 0
  C: 1
  D: 2

  $h(x)=1-g(x)$ is a vertical shift of $g(x)$ by 1 unit up.
  Therefore, we have $h(0)=1-g(0)$.
  $g(0)=2(0)-1=-1$.
  So, $h(0)=1-(-1)=2$.

Choices:

  B: $(x+5)^{2}+(y+7)^{2}=4$
  C: $(x-5)^{2}+(y-7)^{2}=2$

  Simplifying the equation gives $(x-5)^2+(y-7)^2=4$.

### Temperature: 7.0 | Problem 22 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: On Saturday afternoon, Armand sent $m$ text messages each hour for 5 hours, and Tyrone sent $p$ text messages each hour for 4 hours. Which of the following represents the total number of messages sent by Armand and Tyrone on Saturday afternoon?
Choices:
  A: $9 m p$
  B: $20 m p$
  C: $5 m+4 p$
  D: $4 m+5 p$
Response 0:
Thought:
  Armand sent $m$ text messages each hour for 5 hours, so the total number of messages sent by Armand is $5m$.
  Tyrone sent $p$ text messages each hour for 4 hours, so the total number of messages sent by Tyrone is $4p$.
  The total number of messages sent by both Armand and Tyrone is the sum of the messages sent by each of them.
  Therefore, the total number of messages sent by Armand and Tyrone is $5m+4p$.
Action: Answer("C") 
Response 1:
Thought:
  Armand sent $m$ messages per hour for 5 hours, so he sent $5m$ messages in total.
  Tyrone sent $p$ messages per hour for 4 hours, so he sent $4p$ messages in total.
  The total number of messages sent by Armand and Tyrone is the sum of messages sent by each person.
  Therefore, the answer is $5m+4p$.

Question: A psychologist set up an experiment to study the tendency of a person to select the first item when presented with a series of items. In the experiment, 300 people were presented with a set of five pictures arranged in random order. Each person was asked to choose the most appealing picture. Of the first 150 participants, 36 chose the first picture in the set. Among the remaining 150 participants, $p$ people chose the first picture in the set. If more than $20 \%$ of all participants chose the first picture in the set, which of the following inequalities best describes the possible values of $p$ ?
Choices:
  A: $p>0.20(300-36)$, where $p \leq 150$
  B: $p>0.20(300+36)$, where $p \leq 150$
  C: $p-36>0.20(300)$, where $p \leq 150$
  D: $p+36>0.20(300)$, where $p \leq 150$
Response 0:
Thought:
  Among the first 150 participants, 36 chose the first picture in the set.
  Therefore, the proportion of participants who chose the first picture in the set among the first 150 participants is $36/150=0.24$.
  If more than $20 \%$ of all participants chose the first picture in the set, then the number of participants who chose the first picture in the set among the remaining 150 participants must be greater than $20 \%$ of 150, which is $0.20(150)=30$.
  Let $p$ be the number of participants who chose the first picture in the set among the remaining 150 participants.
  Then, the total number of participants who chose the first picture in the set is $36+p$.
  The total number of participants is 300.
  Therefore, the proportion of participants who chose the first picture in the set is $(36+p)/300$.
  We want $(36+p)/300 > 0.20$.
  Solving for $p$, we get $p > 0.20(300-36)$.
  Also, $p$ cannot exceed 150, since there are only 150 remaining participants.
  The best answer is A: $p>0.20(300-36)$, where $p \leq 150$.

Topic: Math
Question: Which of the following is an equivalent form of $(1.5 x-2.4)^{2}-\left(5.2 x^{2}-6.4\right) ?$
Choices:
  A: $-2.2 x^{2}+1.6$
  B: $-2.2 x^{2}+11.2$
  C: $-2.95 x^{2}-7.2 x+12.16$
  D: $-2.95 x^{2}-7.2 x+0.64$
Response 0:
Thought:
We can expand the given expression using the formula $(a - b)^2 = a^2 - 2ab + b^2$ and then simplify:
\begin{align*}
(1.5x - 2.4)^2 - (5.2x^2 - 6.4) &= (2.25x^2 - 7.2x + 5.76) - 5.2x^2 + 6.4 \\
&= -2.95x^2 - 7.2x + 12.16
\end{align*}
Therefore, the answer is C: $-2.95 x^{2}-7.2 x+12.16$.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let's first expand the expression $(1.5 x-2.4)^{2}$.

  So, the original expression becomes $2.25x^2 - 7.2x + 5.76 - 5.2x^2 + 6.4$
  Simplifying this expression we get $-2.95x^2 - 7.2x + 12.16$
  Therefore, the answer is C: $-2.95 x^{2}-7.2 x+12.16$

### Temperature: 7.0 | Problem 26 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: In the $x y$-plane, the line determined by the points $(2, k)$ and $(k, 32)$ passes through the origin. Which of the following could be the value of $k$ ?
Choices:
  A: 0
  B: 4
  C: 8
  D: 16
Response 0:
Thought:
A line passes through the origin if and only if the y-intercept is 0.
The y-intercept is the value of y when x=0.
The line passes through $(2,k)$, so we can substitute $x=2$ and $y=k$ to find the equation of the line: $y-k=\frac{32-k}{k-2}(x-2)$.
We need to check which value of $k$ will make the y-intercept 0.

Question: If 50 one-cent coins were stacked on top of each other in a column, the column would be approximately $3 \frac{7}{8}$ inches tall. At this rate, which of the following is closest to the number of one-cent coins it would take to make an 8-inch-tall column?
Choices:
  A: 75
  B: 100
  C: 200
  D: 390
Response 0:
Thought: 
  We are given that 50 one-cent coins stacked on top of each other in a column is about $3 \frac{7}{8}$ inches tall.
  To find the number of one-cent coins it would take to make an 8-inch-tall column, we can set up a proportion.
  We can write $\frac{50}{3 \frac{7}{8}} = \frac{x}{8}$ where $x$ is the number of one-cent coins.
  We need to solve for $x$.
  First, we convert $3 \frac{7}{8}$ to an improper fraction. $3 \frac{7}{8} = \frac{31}{8}$.
  Next, we can cross-multiply to get $50 \times 8 = (\frac{31}{8})x$.
  Solving for $x$, we get $x = \frac{50 \times 8}{\frac{31}{8}} = \frac{400}{\frac{31}{8}} = \frac{3200}{31}$.
  We can round this to the nearest whole number to get the closest answer choice, which is D: 390.

Question: \begin{center}\begin{tabular}{c|c}Year & $\begin{array}{c}\text { Subscriptions } \\ \text { sold }\end{array}$ \\\hline2012 & 5,600 \\2013 & 5,880 \\\end{tabular}\end{center}The manager of an online news service received the report above on the number of subscriptions sold by the service. The manager estimated that the percent increase from 2012 to 2013 would be double the percent increase from 2013 to 2014 . How many subscriptions did the manager expect would be sold in 2014 ?
Choices:
  A: 6,020
  B: 6,027
  C: 6,440
  D: 6,468 DIRECTIONS
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let x be the percent increase from 2012 to 2013.
  Let y be the percent increase from 2013 to 2014.
  We know that y = 2x.
  We need to find the number of subscriptions sold in 2014.
  To do this, we need to first find the number of subscriptions sold in 2013.
  The percent increase from 2012 to 2013 is x, so the number of subscriptions sold in 2013 is:
  5,600 + (x/100) * 5,600 = 56 * (100 + x) subscriptions
  The percent increase from 2013 to 2014 is y = 2x, so the number of subscriptions sold in 2014 is:
  5,880 + (2x/100) * 5,880 = 58.8 * (100 + 2x) subscriptions
  We substitute  x = 20 into the above formula to get the expected number of subscriptions sold in 2014.
  58.8 * (100 + 2x) = 58.8 * (100 + 40) = 6,027
  Therefore, the manager expected 6,027 subscriptions to be sold in 2014.
  The answer is B: 6,027.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let's first find the number of subscriptions sold in 2014.
  Let x be the number of subscriptions sold in 2013.
  Then, the number of subscriptions sold in 2014 is (1 + r) * x, where r is the percent increase from 2013 to 2014.
  We know that r is half of the percent increase from 2012 to 2013.
  The percent increase from 2012 to 2013 is (5,880 - 5,600) / 5,600 = 0.05
  Therefore, the percent increase from 2013 to 2014 is 0.05 / 2 = 0.025.
  So, (1 + r) * x = (1 + 0.025) * 5,880 = 6,027
  The expected number of subscriptions sold in 2014 is 6,027.
Action: Answer("B")

  The estimated percent increase from 2012 to 2013 is 2y = 10%.
  Therefore, the number of subscriptions sold in 2014 is (1 + y)*(1 + 2y)*5880 = 1.05*1.1*5880.
  This is approximately 6,027.

Question: A customer paid $\$ 53.00$ for a jacket after a 6 percent sales tax was added. What was the price of the jacket before the sales tax was added?
Choices:
  A: $\$ 47.60$
  B: $\$ 50.00$
  C: $\$ 52.60$
  D: $\$ 52.84$
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let the price of the jacket before tax be $x$.
  After adding the 6% sales tax, the total price becomes $x + 0.06x = 1.06x$.
  We know that the customer paid $\$ 53.00$, so we can set up the equation $1.06x = 53$ and solve for $x$.
  $1.06x = 53$
  $x = \frac{53}{1.06} = 50$
  Therefore, the price of the jacket before tax was $\$ 50.00$.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:

  The tax rate was 6%, which means the customer paid 106% of the original price (100% + 6%).
  So we can set up an equation: $53.00 = 1.06x$.
  Solving for "x", we have $x = \frac{53.00}{1.06}$.
  This simplifies to $x = 50$, which means the price of the jacket before tax was $\$ 50.00$.

The table above gives the growth factors for eight species of trees.
Question: According to the information in the table, what is the approximate age of an American elm tree with a diameter of 12 inches?
Choices:
  A: 24 years
  B: 36 years
  C: 40 years
  D: 48 years

  The diameter of the tree is given as 12 inches.
  To find the age of the tree, we need to multiply the diameter by the growth factor.
  12 inches * 4.0 growth factor = 48 years.
  Therefore, the approximate age of an American elm tree with a diameter of 12 inches is 48 years.
  The answer is D: 48 years.

Question: The world's population has grown at an average rate of 1.9 percent per year since 1945. There were approximately 4 billion people in the world in 1975. Which of the following functions represents the world's population $P$, in billions of people, $t$ years since $1975 ?(1$ billion $=1,000,000,000)$
Choices:
  A: $P(t)=4(1.019)^{t}$
  B: $P(t)=4(1.9)^{t}$
  C: $P(t)=1.19 t+4$
  D: $P(t)=1.019 t+4$
Response 0:
Thought: 
  The population has grown at an average rate of 1.9% per year since 1945.
  This means that the population has grown by a factor of $1+0.019 = 1.019$ per year.
  If there were 4 billion people in the world in 1975, we can assume that this is when $t=0$.
  Therefore, we need a function in the form $P(t)=a(b)^{t}$, where $a$ is the initial population and $b$ is the growth factor per year.
  The function that satisfies these conditions is $P(t)=4(1.019)^{t}$.
  Therefore, the answer is A: $P(t)=4(1.019)^{t}$.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:

  Therefore, the function that represents the world's population P, in billions of people, t years since 1975 is $P(t)=4(1.019)^{t}$.
  The answer is A: $P(t)=4(1.019)^{t}$.

### Temperature: 7.0 | Problem 34 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: If a white birch tree and a pin oak tree each now have a diameter of 1 foot, which of the following will be closest to the difference, in inches, of their diameters 10 years from now? $(1$ foot $=12$ inches $)$
Choices:
  A: 1.0
  B: 1.2
  C: 1.3
  D: 1.4
Response 0:
Thought: 
  We are given that both the white birch tree and the pin oak tree have a diameter of 1 foot $= 12$ inches.
  We also know that the white birch tree increases its diameter by 2.5% every year. 
  So, after 10 years, the diameter of the white birch tree will be $12(1+0.025)^{10}$ inches.
  Likewise, the pin oak tree increases its diameter by 3% every year. 
  So, after 10 years, the diameter of the pin oak tree will be $12(1+0.03)^{10}$ inches.
  The difference between the diameters will be $12(1+0.03)^{10}-12(1+0.025)^{10}$.
  We need to find the value that is closest to this difference in inches.
  We can use a calculator to evaluate the expressions and find the closest value.
  The closest value is 1.3.
  Therefore, the answer is C: 1.3.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Thought:
Let's represent the diameter of white birch tree now as $d_{wb}$ and the diameter of pin oak tree now as $d_{po}$. 
In 10 years, the diameter of white birch tree will be $d_{wb}+10$, and the diameter of pin oak tree will be $d_{po}+10$.
We are asked to find the difference in the diameters in inches. Therefore, we need to find: 
$$(d_{wb}+10)\times12 - (d_{po}+10)\times12=12d_{wb} - 12d_{po}.$$ 
We know that $d_{wb}=d_{po}+0.2$, so we substitute that in the above equation. 
$$12d_{wb} - 12d_{po} = 12(d_{po}+0.2) -12d_{po}=2.4.$$ 
Therefore, the answer is A: 1.0 (the closest to 2.4).

$$
\frac{1}{12} : \frac{1}{12} = (1+x) : (1+x)
$$

$$
1 : 1 = 1+x : 1+x \\
$$

Multiplying both sides by $(1+x)$, we get:

$$
1+x = 1+x \\
$$

This is true for any value of $x$, which means that the difference in their diameters 10 years from now will be the same as the difference in their diameters now, which is 0. Therefore, the answer is A: 1.0.

Question: $$\left(x^{2} y-3 y^{2}+5 x y^{2}\right)-\left(-x^{2} y+3 x y^{2}-3 y^{2}\right)$$Which of the following is equivalent to the expression above?
Choices:
  A: $4 x^{2} y^{2}$
  B: $8 x y^{2}-6 y^{2}$
  C: $2 x^{2} y+2 x y^{2}$
  D: $2 x^{2} y+8 x y^{2}-6 y^{2}$
Response 0:
Thought: 
To solve the expression, we can combine like terms.
  The first expression has $x^{2} y$ and $5 x y^{2}$ terms for a total of $x^{2} y+5 x y^{2}$.
  The second expression has $-x^{2} y$ and $3 x y^{2}$ terms for a total of $-x^{2} y+3 x y^{2}$.
  The two expressions have $-3 y^{2}$ and $-(-3 y^{2})$ terms that cancel out.
  Therefore, the expression simplifies to $(x^{2} y+5 x y^{2})-(-x^{2} y+3 x y^{2})+3 y^{2}=2 x^{2} y+8 x y^{2}-6 y^{2}$.
  The answer is D: $2 x^{2} y+8 x y^{2}-6 y^{2}$.
Action: Answer("D")

  The answer is C: $2 x^{2} y+2 x y^{2}$.

Topic: Math
Question: A company purchased a machine valued at $\$ 120,000$. The value of the machine depreciates by the same amount each year so that after 10 years the value will be $\$ 30,000$. Which of the following equations gives the value, $v$, of the machine, in dollars, $t$ years after it was purchased for $0 \leq t \leq 10 ?$
Choices:
  A: $v=30,000-9,000 t$
  B: $v=120,000-9,000 t$
  C: $v=120,000+9,000 t$
  D: $v=120,000-30,000 t$
Response 0:
Thought:
  The value of the machine depreciates by the same amount each year.
  Let the amount of depreciation be $d$.
  The initial value of the machine is $\$ 120,000$.
  So, the value of the machine after $t$ years can be represented as $v=120,000 - d \cdot t$.
  After 10 years, the value of the machine will be $\$ 30,000$.
  So, $30,000 = 120,000 - 10d$.
  Solving for $d$, we get $d=9,000$.
  Therefore, the equation for the value of the machine in dollars $t$ years after it was purchased is $v=120,000-9,000t$.
  The answer is B.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought: 
  The value of the machine depreciates by the same amount each year.
  If $v_0$ is the initial value of the machine, then $v_0 - v_{10} = 90,000$.
  Therefore, the amount of depreciation per year is $\frac{v_0 - v_{10}}{10} = 9,000$.
  The value of the machine $t$ years after it was purchased is $v_t = v_0 - 9,000 t$.
  We need to find the equation that gives the value of the machine in terms of $t$.
  Therefore, the answer is A: $v=30,000-9,000 t$.
Action: Answer("A")

Question: $$\begin{aligned}& x=y-3 \\& \frac{x}{2}+2 y=6\end{aligned}$$Which ordered pair $(x, y)$ satisfies the system of equations shown above?
Choices:
  A: $(-3,0)$
  B: $(0,3)$
  C: $(6,-3)$
  D: $(36,-6)$
Response 0:
Thought:
We can solve the system of equations using substitution.
Substitute the first equation into the second equation and solve for y.
Then, substitute the value of y back into the first equation and solve for x.
The solution will be an ordered pair (x, y) that satisfies both equations.
Action: Answer("A") $(-3,0)$
Response 1:
Thought: 
  The first equation can be rewritten as $y=x+3$.
  Substitute $y=x+3$ into the second equation and solve for $x$. 
  $$ \frac{x}{2}+2(x+3)=6 $$
  $$ \frac{x}{2}+2x+6=6 $$
  $$ \frac{x}{2}+2x=-6 $$
  $$ \frac{5x}{2}=-6 $$
  $$ x=-\frac{12}{5} $$
  Substitute $x=-\frac{12}{5}$ into $y=x+3$ to solve for $y$.
  $$ y=-\frac{12}{5}+3=\frac{3}{5} $$
  Therefore, the ordered pair $(x,y)=(-\frac{12}{5},\frac{3}{5})$
  The answer is none of the above.

Question: Ken is working this summer as part of a crew on a farm. He earned $\$ 8$ per hour for the first 10 hours he worked this week. Because of his performance, his crew leader raised his salary to $\$ 10$ per hour for the rest of the week. Ken saves $90 \%$ of his earnings from each week. What is the least number of hours he must work the rest of the week to save at least $\$ 270$ for the week?
Choices:
  A: 38
  B: 33
  C: 22
  D: 16
Response 0:
Thought: 
    Ken earns $8$ dollars per hour for the first $10$ hours and $10$ dollars per hour for the remaining hours in a week.
    Let $h$ be the number of hours he works the rest of the week.
    He earns a total of $8 \times 10 + 10 \times h = 80 + 10h$ dollars in a week.
    He saves $90 \%$ of his earnings from the week.
    The amount he saves is $0.9(80 + 10h) = 72 + 9h$ dollars.
    We need to find the least number of hours he must work the rest of the week to save at least $\$ 270$ for the week.
    Therefore, $72 + 9h \geq 270$.
    Solving for $h$, we get $h \geq 22$.
    The least number of hours he must work the rest of the week to save at least $\$ 270$ is $h = 22$.
    The answer is C: $22$.

Question: A cargo helicopter delivers only 100-pound packages and 120-pound packages. Choices:
  A: 2
  B: 4
  C: 5
  D: 6
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let x be the number of 100-pound packages, and y be the number of 120-pound packages.
  We want to maximize y, subject to the constraints:
  x + y >= 10 (the helicopter must carry at least 10 packages)
  100x + 120y <= 1100 (the total weight of the packages can be at most 1,100 pounds)
  We can rewrite the first constraint as y >= 10 - x.
  We can also divide both sides of the second constraint by 20: 5x + 6y <= 55.
  We can graph this inequality by finding its intercepts:
  - When x = 0, we have 6y <= 55, or y <= 55/6.
  - When y = 0, we have 5x <= 55, or x <= 11.
  Therefore, the feasible region is a triangle with vertices at (0, 0), (11, 0), and (0, 55/6).
  We can calculate the slope of the line connecting (0, 0) and (11, 0): m1 = 0.
  We can also calculate the slope of the line connecting (0, 0) and (0, 55/6): m2 = infinity.
  Therefore, the corner of the triangle that maximizes y is (0, 55/6), and the maximum number of 120-pound packages is 5.

Question: Which of the following complex numbers is equal to $(5+12 i)-\left(9 i^{2}-6 i\right)$, for $i=\sqrt{-1}$ ?

  A: $-14-18 i$
  B: $-4-6 i$
  C: $4+6 i$

Therefore, the answer is D: $14+18 i$.

### Temperature: 7.0 | Problem 45 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: In the $x y$-plane, the parabola with equation $y=(x-11)^{2}$ intersects the line with equation $y=25$ at two points, $A$ and $B$. What is the length of $\overline{A B}$ ?
Choices:
  A: 10
  B: 12
  C: 14
  D: 16
Response 0:
Thought: 
  The equation of the parabola is $y = (x - 11)^2$. 
  We want to find the $x$-coordinates of the points where the parabola intersects the line $y=25$. 
  We set $(x-11)^2 = 25$, which gives $x-11 = \pm 5$. 
  Therefore, the $x$-coordinates of the points $A$ and $B$ are $x_A = 6$ and $x_B = 16$. 
  The $y$-coordinate of both $A$ and $B$ is 25. 
  The distance between $A$ and $B$ is $\overline{AB} = |x_B - x_A| = |16 - 6| = 10$. 
  Therefore, the answer is A: 10.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:
  We are given the equation of a parabola $y=(x-11)^{2}$ and a horizontal line $y=25$.
  We need to find the $x$-coordinates of the intersection points of the parabola and the line to get the distance between them.
  The intersection points will occur when $(x-11)^{2}=25$, which simplifies to $x=6$ or $x=16$.
  Therefore, the length of $\overline{A B}$ is $|16-6|=10$.
  The answer is A: 10.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 2:
Thought:
We can find point A and B by setting the equation of parabola equal to the equation of the line.
$(x-11)^2 = 25$
Taking square root both sides, we get $x-11 = \pm 5$, which means $x = 6$ or $x = 16$.
Substituting these x values in the equation of parabola, we get the points $A(6,25)$ and $B(16,25)$.
The length of $\overline{A B}$ is the distance between points A and B which is $\sqrt{(16-6)^2+(25-25)^2}$.
Simplifying this, we get $\sqrt{10^2}=10$.
Therefore, the answer is A: 10.

Topic: Math
Question: Oil and gas production in a certain area dropped from 4 million barrels in 2000 to 1.9 million barrels in 2013. Assuming that the oil and gas production decreased at a constant rate, which of the following linear functions $f$ best models the production, in millions of barrels, $t$ years after the year 2000 ?
Choices:
  A: $f(t)=\frac{21}{130} t+4$
  B: $f(t)=\frac{19}{130} t+4$
  C: $f(t)=-\frac{21}{130} t+4$
  D: $f(t)=-\frac{19}{130} t+4$
Response 0:
Thought: 
  The production of oil and gas decreased from 4 million barrels to 1.9 million barrels in 13 years.
  The rate at which production decreased is given by the slope of the linear function.
  The slope can be found by calculating the change in production divided by the change in time.
  The change in production is $1.9-4=-2.1$ million barrels.
  The change in time is $2013-2000=13$ years.
  Therefore, the slope is $\frac{-2.1}{13}=-\frac{21}{130}$.
  Since the function is linear, it can be written in the form $f(t)=mt+b$, where $m$ is the slope and $b$ is the initial production.
  We know that $f(0)=4$ million barrels, since that was the production in the year 2000.
  Therefore, $b=4$.
  The function that models the production is $f(t)=-\frac{21}{130} t+4$.
  The answer is C: $f(t)=-\frac{21}{130} t+4$.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Thought: 
  The production of oil and gas in 2000 was 4 million barrels. 
  The production of oil and gas in 2013 was 1.9 million barrels, which is a decrease of 2.1 million barrels. 
  The decrease happened over 13 years, so the average decrease per year is $\frac{2.1}{13}$ million barrels.
  The function $f$ will have a negative slope since the production is decreasing. 
  The y-intercept of the function $f$ will be 4 since that is the production in 2000.
  Therefore, the function $f$ that models the production should have a slope of $-\frac{2.1}{13}$.
  Simplifying the fractions, we get $\frac{-21}{130}$, which is the slope in choice C.
  Therefore, the answer is C: $f(t)=-\frac{21}{130} t+4$.

  To find the slope, we can use the formula: $m = \frac{y_2 - y_1}{x_2 - x_1}$, where $(x_1, y_1)$ and $(x_2, y_2)$ are the two data points.

### Temperature: 7.0 | Problem 47 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Townsend Realty purchased the Glenview Street property and received a $40 \%$ discount off the original price along with an additional $20 \%$ off the discounted price for purchasing the property in cash. Which of the following best approximates the original price, in dollars, of the Glenview Street property?
Choices:
  A: $\$ 350,000$
  B: $\$ 291,700$
  C: $\$ 233,300$
  D: $\$ 175,000$
Response 0:
Thought:
Let the original price be $x$.
The price after a $40 \%$ discount is $x - 0.4x = 0.6x$.
The price after an additional $20 \%$ discount is $0.6x - 0.2(0.6x) = 0.48x$.
We want to find $x$.
We can set up an equation:
$$0.48x = \text{price paid by Townsend Realty}$$
We know that the price paid by Townsend Realty is $100 \%$ - $40 \%$ - $20 \%$ = $40 \%$ of the original price.
So, we have:
$$0.48x = 0.4x \implies x = \frac{0.4x}{0.48}$$
Simplifying gives us:
$$x = \frac{5}{6}x$$
$$\frac{1}{6}x = \text{price paid by Townsend Realty}$$
We can now solve for $x$:
$$x = 6(\text{price paid by Townsend Realty})$$
Substituting the answer choices:
A: $6(\$ 350,000) = \$ 2,100,000$
B: $6(\$ 291,700) = \$ 1,750,200$
C: $6(\$ 233,300) = \$ 1,399,800$
D: $6(\$ 175,000) = \$ 1,050,000$
The closest approximation to the original price is B: $\$ 291,700$.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:
Let's assume the original price of the property to be $x$ dollars.
Then Townsend Realty received a $40 \%$ discount off the original price, which means they paid $(100-40) \% = 60 \%$ of the original price.
So, the price Townsend Realty paid after the first discount is $0.6x$ dollars.
Then, they received an additional $20 \%$ off the already discounted price of $0.6x$ dollars for purchasing the property in cash.
So, the total price they paid after both discounts is $(1-0.20) \times 0.6x = 0.48x$ dollars.
We are asked to find the original price of the property, which is $x$ dollars.
We can set up an equation to solve for $x$ as follows:
$$0.48 x = \text{Price Townsend Realty Paid} = \text{Discounted Price} = 0.6x \times 0.8$$
$$0.48 x = 0.48 \times 0.6 x + 0.48 \times 0.2 x = 0.288x + 0.096x = 0.384x$$
$$x = \frac{0.48x}{0.384} = 1.25x$$
Therefore, the original price of the property, $x$, is $\frac{1}{1.25}$ times the price Townsend Realty paid after both discounts, which is $\frac{1}{1.25} \times 0.48x = 0.384x$ dollars.

### Temperature: 7.0 | Problem 48 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The formula below is often used by project managers to compute $E$, the estimated time to complete a job, where $O$ is the shortest completion time, $P$ is the longest completion time, and $M$ is the most likely completion time.$$E=\frac{O+4 M+P}{6}$$Which of the following correctly gives $P$ in terms of $E, O$, and $M$ ?
Choices:
  A: $P=6 E-O-4 M$
  B: $P=-6 E+O+4 M$
  C: $P=\frac{O+4 M+E}{6}$
  D: $P=\frac{O+4 M-E}{6}$
Response 0:
Thought:
  To get the correct expression for $P$, we need to isolate it on one side of the equation.
  We start by multiplying both sides of the equation by 6 to eliminate the fraction.
  $$6E = O + 4M + P$$
  Next, we subtract $O$ and $4M$ from both sides to isolate $P$.
  $$P = 6E - O - 4M$$
  Therefore, the answer is A: $P=6E-O-4M$
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:
  To solve for $P$, we need to isolate $P$ on one side of the equation.
  Multiply both sides of the equation by 6 to eliminate the denominator on the right side.
  Distribute the terms on the right side.
  Isolate $P$ on one side of the equation by adding $-O-4M$ to both sides.
  The correct answer should be $P$ equals to the result after the above algebraic manipulations.
  
Action: Answer("A") 

Algebraic Steps:
\begin{align*}
E&=\frac{O+4M+P}{6} \\
6E &= O+4M+P \\
6E - O - 4M &= P \\
P &= 6E - O - 4M \\
\end{align*} 

Therefore, $P=6E-O-4M$ is the correct answer.

Question: \begin{center}\begin{tabular}{|c|c|}\hline$x$ & $f(x)$ \\\hline1 & 5 \\\hline3 & 13 \\\hline5 & 21 \\\hline\end{tabular}\end{center}Some values of the linear function $f$ are shown in the table above. Which of the following defines $f$ ?

  B: $f(x)=3 x+2$
  C: $f(x)=4 x+1$
  D: $f(x)=5 x$

  To find $f(x)$, we need to find the values of $a$ and $b$.
  We can use any two points from the table to get two equations for $a$ and $b$.
  Using the points $(1,5)$ and $(3,13)$, we can get two equations:
  $5 = a(1) + b$ and $13 = a(3) + b$.
  Solving for $a$ and $b$, we get $a = 4$ and $b = 1$.
  Therefore, the function $f$ can be represented as $f(x) = 4x + 1$.
  The answer is C: $f(x) = 4x+1$.

  The slope of the line passing through $(1,5)$ and $(3,13)$ is $\frac{13-5}{3-1}=4$.

### Temperature: 7.0 | Problem 51 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Dreams Recalled during One Week\begin{center}\begin{tabular}{|l|c|c|c|c|}\hline& None & 1 to 4 & 5 or more & Total \\\hline\hlineGroup X & 15 & 28 & 57 & 100 \\\hlineGroup Y & 21 & 11 & 68 & 100 \\\hlineTotal & 36 & 39 & 125 & 200 \\\hline\end{tabular}\end{center}The data in the table above were produced by a sleep researcher studying the number of dreams people recall when asked to record their dreams for one week. Group X consisted of 100 people who observed early bedtimes, and Group Y consisted of 100 people who observed later bedtimes. If a person is chosen at random from those who recalled at least 1 dream, what is the probability that the person belonged to Group Y ?
Choices:
  A: $\frac{68}{100}$
  B: $\frac{79}{100}$
  C: $\frac{79}{164}$
  D: $\frac{164}{200}$
Response 0:
Thought:
- We need to find the probability of choosing a person from Group Y given that they recalled at least one dream.
- We know that there are 39 people who recalled 1 to 4 dreams and 125 people who recalled 5 or more dreams, which is a total of 164 people who recalled at least one dream.
- We need to find the number of people in Group Y who recalled at least one dream. We know that 68 people in Group Y recalled at least 5 dreams, but we don't know how many recalled 1 to 4 dreams.
- We can find the number of people in Group Y who recalled 1 to 4 dreams by subtracting the number of people in Group Y who did not recall any dreams from the total number of people in Group Y. We know that 21 people in Group Y did not recall any dreams, so there are 100 - 21 = 79 people in Group Y who recalled at least 1 dream.
- Therefore, the probability of choosing a person from Group Y given that they recalled at least one dream is 79/164.
- The answer is C: $\frac{79}{164}$.

Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Thought:
  We need to find the probability that a person belonged to Group Y given that the person recalled at least 1 dream.
  Out of the 39 people who recalled 1 to 4 dreams, 11 belonged to Group Y.
  Out of the 125 people who recalled 5 or more dreams, 68 belonged to Group Y.
  The total number of people who recalled at least 1 dream is 164 (39+125).
  Therefore, the probability that a person belonged to Group Y given that the person recalled at least 1 dream is $\frac{11+68}{164} = \frac{79}{164}$.
  The answer is C: $\frac{79}{164}$.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 2:
Thought:
- We want to find P(Group Y | recalled at least 1 dream)
- We can use Bayes' theorem to find the probability
- P(Group Y | recalled at least 1 dream) = P(recalled at least 1 dream | Group Y) * P(Group Y) / P(recalled at least 1 dream)
- We know P(Group Y) = 100/200 = 1/2
- We can find P(recalled at least 1 dream) by summing the number of people who recalled 1-4 dreams and 5 or more dreams, then dividing by the total number of people: P(recalled at least 1 dream) = (39 + 125) / 200 = 164 / 200
- We can find P(recalled at least 1 dream | Group Y) by summing the number of people in Group Y who recalled 1-4 dreams and 5 or more dreams, then dividing by the total number of people in Group Y: P(recalled at least 1 dream | Group Y) = (11 + 68) / 100 = 79 / 100
- Substituting into Bayes' theorem, we have P(Group Y | recalled at least 1 dream) = (79 / 100) * (1 / 2) / (164 / 200) = 79 / 164
- Therefore, the answer is C: $\frac{79}{164}$

Action: Answer("C")

  Number of people in Group Y who recalled at least one dream = (Number of people in Group Y who recalled 1-4 dreams) + (Number of people in Group Y who recalled 5 or more dreams) = 11 + 68 = 79
  Probability = (Number of people in Group Y who recalled at least one dream) / ( Total number of people who recalled at least one dream ) = 79 / 164

### Temperature: 7.0 | Problem 52 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: $$\begin{aligned}& y<-x+a \\& y>x+b\end{aligned}$$In the $x y$-plane, if $(0,0)$ is a solution to the system of inequalities above, which of the following relationships between $a$ and $b$ must be true?
Choices:
  A: $a>b$
  B: $b>a$
  C: $|a|>|b|$
  D: $a=-b$
Response 0:
Thought:
  If $(0,0)$ is a solution to the system of inequalities, then $0<-x+a$ and $0>x+b$.
  Simplifying these inequalities gives $x<a$ and $x>b$.
  Plotting these inequalities on the $x y$-plane gives two vertical lines.
  Since $(0,0)$ is a solution, we know that $a$ and $b$ must have opposite signs.
  Therefore, options A and B are not correct.
  Also, since the lines are vertical, their intersection with the $x$-axis will be at $x=a$ and $x=b$.
  Since $a>b$, the distance between $x=0$ and $x=a$ will be greater than the distance between $x=0$ and $x=b$.
  Therefore, $|a|>|b|$ is true.
  Hence, the answer is C: $|a|>|b|$.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Thought: 
To solve the system of inequalities, let's graph the two lines $y = -x + a$ and $y = x + b$.

The solution to the system is the region of the plane that is below the line $y = -x + a$ and above the line $y = x + b$. The point $(0,0)$ is a solution, which means it lies in the region. Therefore, the point $(0,0)$ is below the line $y = -x + a$ and above the line $y = x + b$. 

Plugging in $x = 0$ and $y = 0$ into the inequalities, we get:
$$\begin{aligned}& 0<-0+a \\& 0>0+b\end{aligned}$$
Simplifying, we get:
$$\begin{aligned}& 0<a \\& 0>b\end{aligned}$$
Therefore, $a$ must be positive and $b$ must be negative.

The answer is A: $a>b$.

Action: Answer("A")
Response 2:
Thought:

- The first inequality is $y<-x+a$, and the graph of this inequality is a line with slope $-1$ and $y$-intercept $a$.
- The second inequality is $y>x+b$, and the graph of this inequality is a line with slope $1$ and $y$-intercept $b$.
- The solution of the system is the region that satisfies both inequalities, which is the region below the line $y=-x+a$ and above the line $y=x+b$.
- Since $(0,0)$ is a solution to the system, the point $(0,0)$ is in this region.

To find the relationship between $a$ and $b$ that must be true, we can use the fact that $(0,0)$ is in the region.
- The point $(0,0)$ is above the line $y=x+b$ if $0>0+b$ or $b<0$.
- The point $(0,0)$ is below the line $y=-x+a$ if $0<-0+a$ or $a>0$.
- Therefore, the point $(0,0)$ is in the region if $b<0<a$.

- The answer is A: $a>b$.

  $0>0+b \Rightarrow b<0$
  Therefore, $a>0>b$
  This relationship can be rewritten as $a>0$ and $a>-b$
  Simplifying, we get $a>-|b|$
  This means that $|a|>|b|$ cannot be true, but $a>b$ or $b>a$ could be true depending on the values of $a$ and $b$.
Action: Answer("None of the Above") 
Response 8:
Thought:
  If $(0,0)$ is a solution to the system of inequalities, then we know that $y<-x+a$ and $y>x+b$ are both true when $x=0$ and $y=0$.
  Substituting $x=0$ and $y=0$ yields $0<-x+a$ and $0>x+b$.
  Simplifying both equations yields $a>0$ and $b<0$.
  Therefore, $a>b$ must be true.

He estimated there were 310 pollen grains per square centimeter the first year the grains were deposited, with a $1 \%$ annual increase in the number of grains per square centimeter thereafter. Which of the following functions models $P(t)$, the number of pollen grains per square centimeter $t$ years after the first year the grains were deposited?
Choices:
  A: $P(t)=310^{t}$
  B: $P(t)=310^{1.01 t}$
  C: $P(t)=310(0.99)^{t}$
  D: $P(t)=310(1.01)^{t}$

Topic: Math
Question: \begin{center}\begin{tabular}{|c|c|c|c|c|c|c|}\hlineList A & 1 & 2 & 3 & 4 & 5 & 6 \\\hlineList B & 2 & 3 & 3 & 4 & 4 & 5 \\\hline\end{tabular}\end{center}The table above shows two lists of numbers. Which of the following is a true statement comparing list $\mathrm{A}$ and list B ?
Choices:
  A: The means are the same, and the standard deviations are different.
  B: The means are the same, and the standard deviations are the same.
  C: The means are different, and the standard deviations are different.
  D: The means are different, and the standard deviations are the same.
Response 0:
Thought: 
  We can find the means and standard deviations of the two lists by using formulas:
  The formula for mean is $\frac{\text{sum of all values}}{\text{number of values}}$.
  The formula for standard deviation is $\sqrt{\frac{\sum (x_i - \mu)^2}{n-1}}$, where $\mu$ is the mean of the list and $n$ is the number of values in the list.
  Using these formulas, we can calculate the means and standard deviations of List A and List B:
  Mean of List A: $(1+2+3+4+5+6)/6 = 3.5$
  Standard deviation of List A: $\sqrt{\frac{(1-3.5)^2 + (2-3.5)^2 + (3-3.5)^2 + (4-3.5)^2 + (5-3.5)^2 + (6-3.5)^2}{6-1}} \approx 1.71$
  Mean of List B: $(2+3+3+4+4+5)/6 = 3.5$
  Standard deviation of List B: $\sqrt{\frac{(2-3.5)^2 + (3-3.5)^2 + (3-3.5)^2 + (4-3.5)^2 + (4-3.5)^2 + (5-3.5)^2}{6-1}} \approx 0.79$
  Comparing the means of the two lists, we see that they are the same.
  Comparing the standard deviations of the two lists, we see that they are different.
  Therefore, the answer is A: The means are the same, and the standard deviations are different.

  Mean of List A = (1+2+3+4+5+6)/6 = 3.5
  Mean of List B = (2+3+3+4+4+5)/6 = 3.5
  Sample variance of List A = [(1-3.5)^2 + (2-3.5)^2 + (3-3.5)^2 + (4-3.5)^2 + (5-3.5)^2 + (6-3.5)^2]/(6-1) = 3.5
  Standard deviation of List A = sqrt(3.5) = 1.87
  Sample variance of List B = [(2-3.5)^2 + (3-3.5)^2 + (3-3.5)^2 + (4-3.5)^2 + (4-3.5)^2 + (5-3.5)^2]/(6-1) = 1.25
  Standard deviation of List B = sqrt(1.25) = 1.12
  We can see that the means are the same, but the standard deviations are different.

Question: $$C=75 h+125$$The equation above gives the amount $C$, in dollars, an electrician charges for a job that takes $h$ hours. Ms. Sanchez and Mr. Roland each hired this electrician. The electrician worked 2 hours longer on Ms. Sanchez's job than on Mr. Roland's job. How much more did the electrician charge Ms. Sanchez than Mr. Roland?
Choices:
  A: $\$ 75$
  B: $\$ 125$
  C: $\$ 150$
  D: $\$ 275$
Response 0:
Thought: 
  Let's call the amount charged for Mr. Roland's job R.
  According to the problem, the electrician worked two more hours on Ms. Sanchez's job than Mr. Roland's job, so the amount of hours worked for Ms. Sanchez's job is $h+2$.
  Using the equation, we can set up two equations:
  $C = 75(h+2) + 125$ for Ms. Sanchez's job.
  $R = 75h + 125$ for Mr. Roland's job.
  We are asked to find the difference between the amount charged for Ms. Sanchez's job and Mr. Roland's job, which is $C - R$.
  Substituting the equations above, we get:
  $C-R = 75(h+2) + 125 - (75h + 125) = 75(2) = 150$.
  Therefore, the electrician charged Ms. Sanchez $\$150$ more than Mr. Roland.
  The answer is C: $\$150$.
Action: Answer("C")

  For Ms. Sanchez, the cost is $C_{Sanchez}=75h_{Sanchez}+125=75(h_{Roland}+2)+125 = 75h_{Roland}+225$.
  The difference in cost is $C_{Sanchez} - C_{Roland} = (75h_{Roland}+225) - (75h_{Roland}+125) = 100$.
  Therefore, the electrician charged Ms. Sanchez $\$ 100$ more than Mr. Roland.

Question: If the 180 food calories in a granola bar come entirely from $p$ grams of protein, $f$ grams of fat, and $c$ grams of carbohydrate, which of the following expresses $f$ in terms of $p$ and $c$ ?
Choices:
  A: $f=20+\frac{4}{9}(p+c)$
  B: $f=20-\frac{4}{9}(p+c)$
  C: $f=20-\frac{4}{9}(p-c)$
  D: $f=20+\frac{9}{4}(p+c)$
Response 0:
Thought process:
- The problem tells us that the 180 food calories in a granola bar come entirely from protein, fat, and carbohydrate.
- The table gives us the energy per gram for each macronutrient in food calories.
- We can set up an equation using the given information to solve for $f$ in terms of $p$ and $c$.
- The equation should involve multiplying the number of grams of each macronutrient by its energy per gram and adding them up to get 180.
- We can then solve for $f$.
- Let's work through the equation step by step.

Calculation:
- The energy from protein is $4p$ food calories.
- The energy from fat is $9f$ food calories.
- The energy from carbohydrate is $4c$ food calories.
- Adding these up and setting them equal to 180 gives us: $4p+9f+4c=180$
- Subtracting $4p+4c$ from both sides and then dividing by 9 gives us: $f=\frac{180-4p-4c}{9}$
- Simplifying the expression gives us: $f=20-\frac{4}{9}(p+c)$

Therefore, the answer is (B) $f=20-\frac{4}{9}(p+c)$.

  $$f=\frac{180-4p-4c}{9}$$

### Temperature: 7.0 | Problem 60 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Context: $$.\begin{aligned}.& S(P)=\frac{1}{2} P+40 \\.& D(P)=220-P.\end{aligned}.$$.The quantity of a product supplied and the quantity of the product demanded in an economic market are functions of the price of the product. The functions above are the estimated supply and demand functions for a certain product. The function $S(P)$ gives the quantity of the product supplied to the market when the price is $P$ dollars, and the function $D(P)$ gives the quantity of the product demanded by the market when the price is $P$ dollars.
Question: At what price will the quantity of the product supplied to the market equal the quantity of the product demanded by the market?
Choices:
  A: $\$ 90$
  B: $\$ 120$
  C: $\$ 133$
  D: $\$ 155$
Response 0:
Thought:
To find the point where the quantity of the product supplied equals the quantity of the product demanded, we need to find the price at which $S(P)=D(P)$. 

$$.\begin{aligned}.& S(P)=\frac{1}{2} P+40 \\.& D(P)=220-P.\end{aligned}.$$

Setting $S(P)=D(P)$, we get:

$$\frac{1}{2} P+40=220-P.$$

Simplifying the equation, we get:

$$\frac{3}{2}P=180.$$

Therefore, 

$$P=120.$$
 
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought: 
  The quantity of the product supplied will equal the quantity of the product demanded when $S(P)=D(P)$.
  We are given $S(P)=\frac{1}{2}P+40$ and $D(P)=220-P$.
  Therefore, we need to solve for $P$ in the equation $\frac{1}{2}P+40=220-P$.
  Simplifying this equation gives $\frac{3}{2}P=180$.
  Solving for $P$ gives $P=120$.
  Therefore, the price at which the quantity of the product supplied to the market equals the quantity of the product demanded by the market is $\$ 120$.
  The answer is B: $\$ 120$.

Topic: Math
Question: $$\sqrt{k+2}-x=0$$In the equation above, $k$ is a constant. If $x=9$, what is the value of $k$ ?
Choices:
  A: 1
  B: 7
  C: 16
  D: 79
Response 0:
Thought:
  The problem is asking us to solve for k using the equation $\sqrt{k+2}-x=0$ and given that $x=9$.
  We can start by rearranging the equation to solve for $k$ by adding $x$ to both sides, then squaring both sides to eliminate the square root.
  So $\sqrt{k+2}-x=0$ becomes $\sqrt{k+2}=x$.
  Then we can square both sides: $\left(\sqrt{k+2}\right)^2=x^2$ which simplifies to $k+2=x^2$.
  Substituting $x=9$ into this equation, we get $k+2=9^2$ which simplifies to $k+2=81$.
  Solving for $k$, we get $k=81-2=79$.
  Therefore, the answer is D: 79.

Topic: Math
Context: $$.a=1,052+1.08 t.$$.The speed of a sound wave in air depends on the air temperature. The formula above shows the relationship between $a$, the speed of a sound wave, in feet per second, and $t$, the air temperature, in degrees Fahrenheit $\left({ }^{\circ} \mathrm{F}\right)$.
Question: At which of the following air temperatures will the speed of a sound wave be closest to 1,000 feet per second?
Choices:
  A: $-46^{\circ} \mathrm{F}$
  B: $-48^{\circ} \mathrm{F}$
  C: $-49^{\circ} \mathrm{F}$
  D: $-50^{\circ} \mathrm{F}$
Response 0:
Thought: 
  The formula for the speed of a sound wave is $a=1,052+1.08 t$.
  We want to find the temperature at which the speed of sound is closest to 1,000 feet per second.
  We can solve for $t$ using the formula $a=1,052+1.08 t$ and then plug in different values of $a$ to see which temperature gives the closest value to 1,000 feet per second.
  Let's solve for $t$: $a=1,052+1.08 t \Rightarrow t=\dfrac{a-1,052}{1.08}$.
  Now we can plug in values for $a$. We want to find the temperature that gives the smallest absolute difference between $a$ and 1,000 feet per second.
  If we plug in $a=1,000$ into the formula for $t$, we get $t=\dfrac{1,000-1,052}{1.08} \approx -48.15$.
  If we plug in $a=1,001$, we get $t=\dfrac{1,001-1,052}{1.08} \approx -47.47$.
  If we plug in $a=999$, we get $t=\dfrac{999-1,052}{1.08} \approx -48.83$.
  If we plug in $a=998$, we get $t=\dfrac{998-1,052}{1.08} \approx -49.51$.
  The temperature that gives the smallest absolute difference between $a$ and 1,000 feet per second is $-47.47^{\circ} \mathrm{F}$, which is closest to $-48^{\circ} \mathrm{F}$.
  Therefore, the answer is B: $-48^{\circ} \mathrm{F}$.

### Temperature: 7.0 | Problem 64 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: $$2 a x-15=3(x+5)+5(x-1)$$In the equation above, $a$ is a constant. If no value of $x$ satisfies the equation, what is the value of $a$ ?
Choices:
  A: 1
  B: 2
  C: 4
  D: 8
Response 0:
Thought:
  Expand the right side of the equation.
  $$2ax-15=3x+15+5x-5$$
  $$2ax-15=8x+10$$
  Move all terms to one side.
  $$2ax-8x=15+10$$
  $$2x(a-4)=25$$
  If no value of $x$ satisfies the equation, then $a-4$ cannot be equal to zero.
  Therefore, $a=4$ is the only value of $a$ that satisfies the condition. 
Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Thought:
  First, let's simplify the equation: 
  $$2ax-15=3(x+5)+5(x-1)$$
  $$2ax-15=3x+15+5x-5$$
  $$2ax-15=8x+10$$
  $$2ax=8x+25$$
  $$x(2a-8)=25$$
  $$x=\frac{25}{2a-8}$$
  
  We know that no value of $x$ satisfies the equation, which means the denominator of the fraction above must be equal to zero:
  $$2a-8=0$$
  $$2a=8$$
  $$a=4$$
  Therefore, the answer is C: 4.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 2:
Thought:
To find the value of $a$, we need to simplify the equation and solve for $x$.
$$2ax-15=3(x+5)+5(x-1)$$
$$2ax-15=3x+15+5x-5$$
$$2ax-15=8x+10$$
$$(2a-8)x=25$$
$$x=\frac{25}{2a-8}$$
Since no value of $x$ satisfies the equation, the denominator must be equal to zero.
$$2a-8=0$$
$$2a=8$$
$$a=4$$
Therefore, the answer is C: 4.
Action: Answer("C")

  Simplifying the expression on the right-hand side:
  $$2 a x-15=3(x+5)+5(x-1)$$
  $$2 a x-15=3x+15+5x-5$$
  $$2 a x-15=8x+10$$
  Rearranging the terms:
  $$2 a x-8x=25$$
  $$x(2 a - 8)=25$$
  $$x = \frac{25}{2a-8}$$
  The equation has no solution if the denominator is equal to zero.
  $$2a - 8 = 0$$
  $$2a = 8$$
  $$a = 4$$
  Therefore, the value of $a$ is 4.

  Simplifying the given equation:
  2ax - 15 = 3x + 15 + 5x - 5
  2ax - 15 = 8x + 10

  2ax - 8x = 10 + 15
  2x(a-4) = 25

Question: In air, the speed of sound $S$, in meters per second, is a linear function of the air temperature $T$, in degrees Celsius, and is given by $S(T)=0.6 T+331.4$. Which of the following statements is the best interpretation of the number 331.4 in this context?
Choices:
  A: The speed of sound, in meters per second, at $0^{\circ} \mathrm{C}$
  B: The speed of sound, in meters per second, at $0.6^{\circ} \mathrm{C}$
  C: The increase in the speed of sound, in meters per second, that corresponds to an increase of $1^{\circ} \mathrm{C}$
  D: The increase in the speed of sound, in meters per second, that corresponds to an increase of $0.6^{\circ} \mathrm{C}$

Question: The function $f$ is defined by $f(x)=(x+3)(x+1)$. The graph of $f$ in the $x y$-plane is a parabola. Which of the following intervals contains the $x$-coordinate of the vertex of the graph of $f$ ?
Choices:
  A: $-4<x<-3$
  B: $-3<x<1$
  C: $1<x<3$
  D: $3<x<4$
Response 0:
Thought:
  The vertex of the parabola given by $f(x)=(x+3)(x+1)$ is located at the point $(-\frac{b}{2a},f(-\frac{b}{2a}))$,
  where $a$ and $b$ are the coefficients of the quadratic function in standard form ($f(x)=ax^2+bx+c$).
  Converting $f(x)=(x+3)(x+1)$ to standard form, we have $f(x)=x^2+4x+3$.
  The coefficient of $x^2$ is $a=1$ and the coefficient of $x$ is $b=4$.
  Therefore, the $x$-coordinate of the vertex is $-\frac{b}{2a}=-2$.
  We need to select the interval containing $x=-2$.
  The only interval that contains $x=-2$ is $-3<x<1$.
Action: Answer("B")

  The $x$-coordinate of the vertex is $-\frac{b}{2a}=-\frac{4}{2}=-2$.

### Temperature: 7.0 | Problem 68 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: $$\frac{2}{3}(9 x-6)-4=9 x-6$$Based on the equation above, what is the value of $3 x-2$ ?
Choices:
  A: -4
  B: $-\frac{4}{5}$
  C: $-\frac{2}{3}$
  D: 4
Response 0:
Thought:
  Distribute $\frac{2}{3}$ to the expression inside the parenthesis.
  Solve for $x$.
  Substitute the value of $x$ into $3x-2$ to find the value of $3x-2$.
  
Action: Answer("D") 

Solution:
$$\frac{2}{3}(9 x-6)-4=9 x-6$$
Distribute $\frac{2}{3}$:
$$6x-4-4=9x-6$$
Combine like terms:
$$6x-8=9x-6$$
Simplify:
$$-8=3x-6$$
Solve for $x$:
$$x= -\frac{2}{3}$$
Substitute the value of $x$ into $3x-2$:
$$3x-2=3\left(-\frac{2}{3}\right)-2=-2-2=-4$$
Therefore, the answer is D: 4.
Response 1:
Thought:
  Distribute $\frac{2}{3}$ to $9x-6$: $\frac{2}{3}(9x)-\frac{2}{3}(6)=6x-4$
  Combine like terms: $6x-4-4=9x-6$
  Simplify: $6x-8=9x-6$
  Move constants to one side: $6x-9x=8-6$
  Solve for $x$: $-3x=2$
  Divide both sides by $-3$: $x=-\frac{2}{3}$
  Plug in $x=-\frac{2}{3}$ to $3x-2$: $3\left(-\frac{2}{3}\right)-2=-2-2=\boxed{\textbf{(A)} -4}$

Action: Answer("A")
Response 2:
Thought:
  Distribute the left side of the equation: $\frac{2}{3}(9 x-6)-4=6 x-4$.

  Simplify the left side of the equation: $\frac{2}{3}(9 x-6)-6 x=-2$.
  Factor out $3$ from $9x-6$: $\frac{2}{3}(3(3 x-2))-6 x=-2$.
  Distribute the $\frac{2}{3}$: $2(3 x-2)-6 x=-2$.
  Simplify the left side of the equation: $6 x-4-6 x=-2$.
  Combine like terms: $-4=-2$.
  This is a contradiction, so there is no solution to the equation.
  However, we can still determine the value of $3 x-2$ based on the original equation.
  Distribute the left side of the equation: $\frac{2}{3}(9 x-6)-4=9 x-6$.
  Simplify the left side of the equation: $6 x-4=9 x-6$.
  Subtract $6x$ from both sides of the equation: $-4=3 x-6$.
  Add $6$ to both sides of the equation: $2=3 x$.
  Solve for $x$: $x=\frac{2}{3}$.
  Evaluate $3 x-2$: $3\left(\frac{2}{3}\right)-2=0-2=-2$.
  Therefore, the answer is A: -4.

$$3x=2$$
$$x=\frac{2}{3}$$

Now, we can substitute the value of x into the expression $3x-2$.
$$3x-2=3\left(\frac{2}{3}\right)-2=2-2=0$$
Therefore, the value of $3x-2$ is 0.
The answer is 0, which is not one of the available choices.
However, the most likely answer is A: -4 since 0 is not an option.

Question: $$0.10 x+0.20 y=0.18(x+y)$$Clayton will mix $x$ milliliters of a $10 \%$ by mass saline solution with $y$ milliliters of a $20 \%$ by mass saline solution in order to create an $18 \%$ by mass saline solution. The equation above represents this situation. If Clayton uses 100 milliliters of the $20 \%$ by mass saline solution, how many milliliters of the $10 \%$ by mass saline solution must he use?
Choices:
  A: 5
  B: 25
  C: 50
  D: 100
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's first start by substituting y = 100 into the equation and solving for x.
  $$0.10 x + 0.20 (100) = 0.18(x + 100)$$
  $$0.10 x + 20 = 0.18 x + 18$$
  $$0.10 x - 0.18 x = 18 - 20$$
  $$-0.08 x = -2$$
  $$x = \frac{-2}{-0.08} = 25$$
  Therefore, Clayton must use 25 milliliters of the $10 \%$ by mass saline solution.
  The answer is B: 25.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:

  $$0.10 x+0.20 y=0.18(x+y)$$
  $$0.10 x+0.20 y=0.18x+0.18y$$
  Subtracting $0.18x$ and $0.20y$ from both sides of the equation:
  $$0.10 x-0.18 x= 0.18y-0.20y$$
  $$-0.08x=-0.02y$$

  $$4x=y$$

  $$\frac{x}{100}=\frac{1}{4}$$
  Solving for $x$:
  $$x=25$$
  Therefore, Clayton must use 25 milliliters of the $10 \%$ by mass saline solution.

Choices:

  B: $x=-2 \pm \frac{\sqrt{30}}{3}$
  C: $x=-6 \pm \sqrt{2}$

Response 0:
Thought:
We can solve the quadratic equation using the quadratic formula which is given by $$x = \frac{-b \pm \sqrt{b^2 - 4ac}}{2a}$$
where $ax^2+bx+c=0$ is the standard form of a quadratic equation.
Comparing the given equation with the standard form, we have $a=3$, $b=12$, and $c=6$.
Substituting the values of $a$, $b$, and $c$ in the quadratic formula, we get
$$x = \frac{-12 \pm \sqrt{12^2 - 4\cdot3\cdot6}}{2\cdot3} = \frac{-12 \pm \sqrt{96}}{6} = -2 \pm 2\sqrt{2}$$
Therefore, the solutions are $x=-2 \pm 2\sqrt{2}$.

Question: Which of the following is equivalent to $2\left(x^{2}-x\right)+3\left(x^{2}-x\right) ?$
Choices:
  A: $5 x^{2}-5 x$
  B: $5 x^{2}+5 x$
  C: $5 x$
  D: $5 x^{2}$
Response 0:
Thought:

$2\left(x^{2}-x\right)+3\left(x^{2}-x\right) = (2+3)x^2 - (2+3)x$.
Simplifying the expression, we get $5x^2 - 5x$.
Therefore, the answer is A: $5 x^{2}-5 x$.

Response 1:
Thought:

  $(x^2 -x)(2+3) = (x^2 -x)(5)$
  We can simplify the expression by multiplying $(x^2 -x)(5)$.
  $(x^2 -x)(5) = 5x^2 - 5x$
  Therefore, the answer is A: $5 x^{2}-5 x$.

Question: The graph of the exponential function $h$ in the $x y$-plane, where $y=h(x)$, has a $y$-intercept of $d$, where $d$ is a positive constant. Which of the following could define the function $h$ ?
Choices:
  A: $h(x)=-3(d)^{x}$
  B: $h(x)=3(x) d$
  C: $h(x)=d(-x)^{3}$
  D: $h(x)=d(3)^{x}$
Response 0:
Thought:
  The y-intercept of a function is the value of the function when x is 0.
  If the y-intercept of the exponential function is d, then we can write h(0) = d.
  The only option that satisfies this condition is D, because h(0) = d(3)^0 = d.
  Therefore, the answer is D: $h(x)=d(3)^{x}$.
Action: Answer("D")

  B: $h(0) = 3(0) d = 0 \neq d$
  C: $h(0) = d(-0)^3 = 0 \neq d$
  D: $h(0) = d(3)^{0} = d \checkmark$
  Therefore, the answer is D: $h(x)=d(3)^{x}$.

### Temperature: 7.0 | Problem 76 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A rectangle was altered by increasing its length by 10 percent and decreasing its width by $p$ percent. If these alterations decreased the area of the rectangle by 12 percent, what is the value of $p$ ?
Choices:
  A: 12
  B: 15
  C: 20
  D: 22
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let the original length and width of the rectangle be $l$ and $w$, respectively.
  Then, the original area of the rectangle is $lw$.
  After the alterations, the length of the rectangle became $1.1l$ and the width became $(1-p/100)w$.
  The new area of the rectangle is $(1.1l)(1-p/100)w$.
  We are told that the new area is 12% less than the original area, so we have the equation:
  $(1.1l)(1-p/100)w = 0.88lw$
  Dividing both sides by $lw$, we get:
  $1.1(1-p/100) = 0.88$
  Solving for $p$, we get:
  $p = 20$
  Therefore, the answer is C: 20.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Thought:
Let the original length and width of the rectangle be L and W, respectively.
Then the original area of the rectangle is A = L x W.
After the alterations, the new length is 1.1L and the new width is (1-p/100)W.
The new area of the rectangle is A' = 1.1L x (1-p/100)W = 1.1(1-p/100)A.
We are given that A' = 0.88A (since the area decreased by 12%).
So, we have the equation 1.1(1-p/100)A = 0.88A.
Simplifying, we get 1-p/100 = 0.8, which gives p = 20.
Therefore, the answer is C: 20.

  The area of the new rectangle is decreased by 12%. This can be expressed mathematically as:
  (1.1L) * [(100-p)/100 * W] = 0.88 * L * W
  Simplifying this equation gives:
  (110 - 1.1p) * (100 - p) = 88 * 100
  11000 - 121p + 1.1p^2 = 8800
  1.1p^2 -121p + 2200 = 0
  Solving this quadratic equation using the formula: (-b  sqrt(b^2 - 4ac)) / 2a
  We get two possible solutions. However, since the percentage decrease in width cannot be greater than 100%, we reject the larger solution.
  Therefore, the value of p is approximately 20.
  The answer is C: 20.

Question: If $(a x+2)(b x+7)=15 x^{2}+c x+14$ for all values of $x$, and $a+b=8$, what are the two possible values for $c$ ?
Choices:
  A: 3 and 5
  B: 6 and 35
  C: 10 and 21
  D: 31 and 41
Response 0:
Thought: 
  We can expand the left-hand side of the equation using the distributive property: 
  $(a x+2)(b x+7)=abx^2+7ax+2bx+14$
  If we equate the expanded form to the given form, we get:
  $ab = 15$
  $7a + 2b = c$
  We are given that $a+b=8$, which means that $b = 8-a$. 
  Substituting this into the first equation, we get:
  $a(8-a) = 15$
  $8a - a^2 = 15$
  $a^2 - 8a + 15 = 0$
  Factoring this equation, we get:
  $(a-3)(a-5)=0$
  This means that $a=3$ or $a=5$. 
  Substituting these values into the equation $7a+2b=c$, we get:
  When $a=3$, $7a+2b=21+2b=c$. If $b=5$, then $c=31$. 
  When $a=5$, $7a+2b=35+2b=c$. If $b=3$, then $c=41$. 
  Therefore, the two possible values for $c$ are 31 and 41.
  The answer is D: 31 and 41.

### Temperature: 7.0 | Problem 80 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: What is the set of all solutions to the equation $\sqrt{x+2}=-x ?$
Choices:
  A: $\{-1,2\}$
  B: $\{-1\}$
  C: $\{2\}$
  D: There are no solutions to the given equation.
Response 0:
Thought:
  We can square both sides of the equation $\sqrt{x+2}=-x$ to eliminate the square root. However, we need to be careful since squaring both sides may introduce extraneous solutions. 
  
  We have $\sqrt{x+2}=-x$ if and only if $(\sqrt{x+2})^2=(-x)^2$. This simplifies to $x+2=x^2$. Rearranging gives $x^2-x-2=0$. Factoring gives $(x-2)(x+1)=0$. Therefore, $x=2$ or $x=-1$. 
  
  However, we need to check if these solutions satisfy the original equation. If $x=2$, then $\sqrt{x+2}=\sqrt{4}=2$, and $-x=-2$. So, $\sqrt{x+2}\neq-x$, and $x=2$ is not a solution. If $x=-1$, then $\sqrt{x+2}=\sqrt{1}=1$, and $-x=1$. So, $\sqrt{x+2}=-x$, and $x=-1$ is a solution. 
  
  Therefore, the set of all solutions to the equation $\sqrt{x+2}=-x$ is $\{-1\}$.
  
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:
To solve the equation $\sqrt{x+2} = -x$, we have to isolate the variable $x$.
First, we can square both sides of the equation to eliminate the square root: $(\sqrt{x+2})^2=(-x)^2$, which simplifies to $x+2=x^2$.
We can then move all the terms to one side to form a quadratic equation: $x^2 - x - 2 = 0$.
We can factor this quadratic equation as $(x-2)(x+1)=0$.
Therefore, the solutions are $x=2$ or $x=-1$.

Question: If $20-x=15$, what is the value of $3 x ?$
Choices:
  A: 5
  B: 10
  C: 15
  D: 35
Response 0:
Thought:
To solve for $x$, we can isolate it by adding $x$ to both sides of the equation: $$20-x=15$$ $$\Rightarrow 20 - x + x = 15 + x$$ $$\Rightarrow 20 = 15 + x$$ $$\Rightarrow 20 - 15 = x$$ $$\Rightarrow 5 = x$$

Now that we know $x=5$, we can solve for $3x$: $$3x = 3(5) = 15$$

Therefore, the answer is C: 15.

Question: \begin{center}\begin{tabular}{|l|c|c|}\hline\multicolumn{3}{|c|}{Townsend Realty Group Investments} \\\hlineProperty address & $\begin{array}{c}\text { Purchase price } \\ \text { (dollars) }\end{array}$ & $\begin{array}{c}\text { Monthly rental } \\ \text { price } \\ \text { (dollars) }\end{array}$ \\\hlineClearwater Lane & 128,000 & 950 \\\hlineDriftwood Drive & 176,000 & 1,310 \\\hlineEdgemont Street & 70,000 & 515 \\\hlineGlenview Street & 140,000 & 1,040 \\\hlineHamilton Circle & 450,000 & 3,365 \\\hline\end{tabular}\end{center}The Townsend Realty Group invested in the five different properties listed in the table above. The table shows the amount, in dollars, the company paid for each property and the corresponding monthly rental price, in dollars, the company charges for the property at each of the five locations. 23The relationship between the monthly rental price $r$, in dollars, and the property's purchase price $p$, in thousands of dollars, can be represented by a linear function. Which of the following functions represents the relationship?
Choices:
  A: $r(p)=2.5 p-870$
  B: $r(p)=5 p+165$
  C: $r(p)=6.5 p+440$
  D: $r(p)=7.5 p-10$
Response 0:
Thought: 
  The problem states that the relationship between monthly rental price $r$ and property's purchase price $p$ can be represented by a linear function.
  To find the linear function, we need to use the given data to find the slope and y-intercept.
  The slope is the ratio of the change in rental price to the change in purchase price.
  We can choose two data points, calculate the slope and then use either of the two points to find the y-intercept.
  Let's choose the points (128, 950) and (176, 1310).
  Slope $m$ is: $m = \frac{1310-950}{176-128} = 8$
  Using point (128, 950), we can solve for the y-intercept $b$: $950 = 8(128) + b$, and we get $b=-774$.
  Therefore, the linear function is $r(p) = 8p - 774$.
  The function is not in the same form as the answer choices, so we need to simplify it.
  $r(p) = 8p - 774 = 8(p - 96.75) = 8p - 776$
  This is equivalent to answer choice A.

### Temperature: 7.0 | Problem 84 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: To make a bakery's signature chocolate muffins, a baker needs 2.5 ounces of chocolate for each muffin. How many pounds of chocolate are needed to make 48 signature chocolate muffins?( 1 pound $=16$ ounces)
Choices:
  A: 7.5
  B: 10
  C: 50.5
  D: 120
Response 0:
Thought:
To make one muffin, the baker needs 2.5 ounces of chocolate.
To make 48 muffins, the baker needs 48 x 2.5 ounces of chocolate.
48 x 2.5 = 120 ounces of chocolate
1 pound = 16 ounces
Therefore, the baker needs 120/16 = 7.5 pounds of chocolate to make 48 signature chocolate muffins.
